<review>I first met Dr. Kelly and her staff at the Spring Forward 5K/10K run in Mountain View in 2015.  At that time, I had a concern about chiropractic care because people that I knew who regularly saw a chiropractor seemed "addicted" to it:  that is to say that at times they didn't feel right unless they saw the chiropractor regularly.  I didn't want to get into a codependent habit.  I figured if I stretched, stayed limber, got a massage once a month and just did common sense things, I would never need to.

But I was all to happy to get the free 15 minute massage that their booth offered and leave it at that.

Later that same year, I experienced actual shoulder and back pain that wouldn't go away.  And I realized that I was just medicating it with pain killers and waiting for it to go away, like you would when you see your personal physician.  That didn't seem healthy either, and I didn't want to get to the point where more powerful muscle relaxants would be needed.  I figured I would give it a shot, and trust my own willpower to discipline myself to only go when I needed to.

But upon visiting her office and meeting her staff, I was shown the videos and learned about vertebral subluxation and its effects.  And through the process, my first experience of being adjusted, and the way that the pain was actually treated instead of waited out, I came to understand the value and purpose of chiropractic and its preventative benefits in avoiding bigger, more painful, and more expensive orthopedic medicine.

When the pain went away, I stopped going just as I planned.  Personal care isn't necessarily cheap:  grooming, pampering, hobbies or activities.  I wanted to only invest what I needed in what I needed.

But through the journey, I also developed a more active lifestyle.  Not that I became a gym rat, but free of pain I found myself being more outdoorsey.  And in the course of time, I developed pain again.  Over time I'd experienced pain (although less severe) from doing stuff:  playing golf, or riding my bike more after not riding for a while and having back pain from being hunched over handlebars, or stiffness from maintaining posture when I rollerblade for the first time in months.  But then, I found myself lifting stuff and doing stuff while cleaning my storage and my apartment, and tweaked my back to where it was actually painful.

And I went back to Dr. Kelly, and once again the pain was treated.  And now I understand the reality of what I used to fear.  Maintenance is less painful than remediation; and in the long run less expensive.

So today it is part of my personal care regimen.  I've adjusted my FSA and chosen my open enrollment to more easily accommodate the healthy habit.  If I tweak something while doing my normal stuff, it is caught early and treated early before it becomes seriously painful or expensive to treat with therapy or medications.

That perhaps speaks to the value of chiropractic care, but then becomes the question of choosing a practitioner that works for you.  Here's where Dr. Kelly and her staff really shine.  Between being both knowledgeable, professional, and personable I have found them to be the perfect partners in maintaining my health.  I had developed the mentality, when I got over my fear of going to doctors or dentists, that what works best for me is to have teammates in maintaining my wellness.  I really do feel like we're on the same team.  When it has been prudent or necessary to re-evaluate practitioners based on my insurance network coverages and whatnot, this is one concession I would not make.

Realities have forced me to change primary care physicians before, when my employer's insurance programs differ.  I've always been dissatisfied with that process.  And so in this case, where I see the chiropractor more times per year than my primary care physician, it doesn't make sense to me to roll the dice.

And so fast forward four years, I can say that I am happily a patient of Dr. Kelly; and I have no fear of doing things knowing that I've got teammates on my side.</review><Pictures>None< /Pictures><Response>{'time': 1575330414303, 'text': "Thank you so much for sharing your experience, Alvin! That alone speaks volumes on how much Dr. Kelly cares for her patients wellness, especially for those of us that walk in experiencing extreme pain. I'm just going to quickly offer my story in case anyone in experiencing pain is looking for a chiropractic center that will take great care of you.

Two weeks ago, when I first walked in to her office, I could barely walk without experiencing excruciating shooting back pain every step of the way. I could barely sit down, and every time I stood up I had to wait 3 minutes before I could stand up straight. I had back pain that I just ignored thinking it would just go away on its own, but this time it just got worse and worse. By the time I started seeing Dr. Kelly my back was a mess, the muscles were really inflamed and would spasm at any mere light touch.

The first two consultation visits were very informative. Dr. Kelly likes to make sure her patients are well-informed, so you get mini tutorials on what a healthy spine looks like, common spine issues, and chiropractic care. She is thorough and realistic about the limitations of our body - especially a body in pain - and is honest with patients about what they can expect with progress.

She was very gentle and very careful with my incredibly pained muscles. She kinesio-taped my back to offer extra support and gave me instructions for home care until my visit the next day. That night she personally called me to check in on me because I had been in so much pain. I felt really cared for.

The next day she did a few adjustments to re-position a vertebrae that was out of place, and I could feel immediate relief. For the first time in weeks I could actually walk without feeling the shooting pains. Again, Dr. Kelly gave me instructions for home care until my visit the next day. Unfortunately, my back was so unstable that accidentally I popped it back out of place pretty much as soon as I left the office.

I toughed the excruciating pain out until my visit the next day, but as soon as I got there the next day, Dr. Kelly told me that I should have called and they could have figured out how to help me, and encouraged me to call if something like that ever happened again. I didn't even think to do that because it's so unusual to experience that level of care. So, she re-positioned that vertebrae again, taught me the proper way to move to avoid popping it back out of place, and this time it stayed.

I continued to see Dr. Kelly one more time that first week, and then 3 times this past week . Each visit of adjustments restored more and more of my range of motion and reduced my pain level. Each time she taped my back to offer extra support. After my third visit this week, l I accidentally popped my vertebrae back out again and I could feel some of the old pressure return. I called Dr. Kelly's office and they squeezed me back in even though I had just been in the office 5 hours earlier. Then, she squeezed me back in for a follow up 2 days later to make sure everything had stayed in place.

Now, two weeks later, I am experiencing no pain. I still don't quite have restored full range of motion, but it's improving day by day, and I can do many things that I have not been able to do in weeks. I know full recovery is going to be a long process.

I highly recommend Dr. Kelly for chiropractic care. Her office is a clean, bright and calming place to go to, her front office staff is cheerful and friendly. She is a doctor that cares first and foremost for her patient's wellness.</Text></record>

< text>
I have been insured by State Farm Insurance for over ten years and just recently I had my car, which is a convertible Toyota Solara, vandalized. The convertible top was ripped horribly and the right side passenger window was shattered with glass sprawled everywhere. To top it off it apparently happened on New Years while I was out of town. As soon as I became aware of the situation I contacted Kim Whippie. She immediately provided me with the information I needed to begin my claim. Once my claim was submitted I was scheduled for a vehicle inspection. The inspector provided the estimate and I was handed a check for the damages. I was also given a detailed list of the companies that provided State Farm with the estimates. Thereafter, I took my car in for repair, only to find out additional issues were identified. The repair shop contacted State Farm and another inspection was scheduled within a few days. After the 2nd inspection State Farm approved of the additional repairs and issued another check directly to the company repairing my car. Overall I just want to say that State Farm is the most professional and prompt insurance company that I have ever worked with.
